Hi all,

So here's a beta version of the new build script I'm working on. It 
builds, Mono, libgdiplus, and cocoa-sharp.

Things still to be done:

    add getopt support to better specify options at command line
    add build from SVN support
    Switch to Python???


Uncompress the attached tgz archive and cd to the macos directory. Then do:

./newbuild.sh YES YES YES $PWD

The three yeses are: 1. configure, 2. make, 3. make install.  The $PWD 
is the location of the resources that are contained in this archive.

Feel free to look it over and make comments.
